-- Tabellenstruktur für Tabelle `drivers`
--

CREATE TABLE `drivers` (
  `id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `ingame_driver_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `first_name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `last_name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `age` tinyint(3) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `skill_val` smallint(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `reliability_val` smallint(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `adr_permit` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `penalty_points` tinyint(3) UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
  `salary` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `is_employed` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 1,
  `assigned_truck_id` int(10) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Tabellenstruktur für Tabelle `market_history`

CREATE TABLE `market_history` (
  `id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `ingame_vehicle_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `location_label` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `vehicle_type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `capacity_t` smallint(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `year_built` smallint(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `km_stand` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `condition_pct` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL,
  `price` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL,
  `tuning_value_total` int(10) UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
  `roi_score` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `recorded_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Tabellenstruktur für Tabelle `orders`
--

CREATE TABLE `orders` (
  `id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `ingame_order_id` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `fingerprint` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `freight_type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `commodity` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `is_adr` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `weight_total` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `weight_remaining` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `revenue` decimal(12,2) NOT NULL,
  `from_city_id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `to_city_id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `is_accepted` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `is_archived` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `assigned_truck_id` int(10) UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `assigned_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_seen_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `completed_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

--
-- Tabellenstruktur für Tabelle `trucks`
--

CREATE TABLE `trucks` (
  `id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `ingame_vehicle_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `user_label` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `vehicle_type` enum('Kurier','Stückgut','Schüttgut','Pritsche','Plane','Koffer','Kühlwagen','Silo','Tankwagen','Schwertransport','ISO-Container','Super-Liner') NOT NULL,
  `capacity_t` smallint(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `year_built` smallint(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `km_stand` int(10) UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
  `current_city_id` int(10) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `has_tuning_motor` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `has_tuning_aero` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `has_tuning_stau` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `is_active_planning` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `is_focussed` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `assigned_driver_id` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Verknuepfung zur ingame_driver_id des Fahrers'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
